***batten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:batten.html>batten</a> (71073)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Debated. A comparable form <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> synonymous <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:baten.html>baten</a></i>, which pertains to the Germanic root at hand in <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:batten.html>batten</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">better</i>. At least a secondary relation with this Dutch verb seems certain. However, its regular cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">bazzen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:batten.html>batten</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which would have <a href = vnd.unilang:led.html>led</a> to modern <i>*<a href = vnd.unilang:bassen.html>bassen</a>, bässen</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:meren.html>Mere</a> borrowing from Low German or Dutch <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unlikely since the verb <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <i>-t-</i> in western Upper German and a corresponding <i>-d-</i> in many dialects of West Central German. Possibly two distinct roots have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> merged.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_3">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:batten.html>batten</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn" lang="de">battet</b>, <i>past tense</i> <b class="Latn" lang="de">battete</b>, <i>past participle</i> <b class="Latn" lang="de">gebattet</b>, <i>auxiliary</i> <b class="Latn" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:haben.html>haben</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> western Germany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be useful, to be of use, to help</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="de">nutzen</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="de">nützen</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:batten.html>batten</a></b> <sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>

<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(sport)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> wicket <a href = vnd.unilang:verdedigen.html>verdedigen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> cricket</li>
<li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(sport)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> bat <a href = vnd.unilang:slaan.html>slaan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> cricket</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lichaamsdeel.html>lichaamsdeel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kompressen.html>kompressen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bevochtigen.html>bevochtigen</a></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Verwante_begrippen"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:verwante.html>Verwante</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:begrippen.html>begrippen</a></i></span></h5>
<ul><li>cricket</li></ul>
</body> 
***batterij.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:batterij.html>batterij</a> (6321)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">batterie</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:batterij.html>batterij</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:batterijen.html>batterijen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:batterijtje.html>batterijtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> battery, tactical artillery unit</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">technology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> electrical battery, power storage device</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:baum.html>baum</a> (30713)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">boum</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*baumaz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:baum.html>Baum</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boom.html>boom</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">beam</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="gsw"><a href = vnd.unilang:baum.html>baum</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span>

***baviaan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:baviaan.html>baviaan</a> (16414)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">baubijn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>. The spelling with <i>-iaen</i> (modern spelling: <i>-iaan</i>) first appears in the sixteenth century, becoming common in the seventeenth century, perhaps due to the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arminian_controversy" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Arminian controversy">Arminian controversy</a>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:baviaan.html>baviaan</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bavianen.html>bavianen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:baviaan.html>baviaantje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">baboon</span>, monkey of the genus <i>Papio</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> Protestantism<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">Arminian</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">Remonstrant</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">mantelbaviaan</span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:baviaan.html>baviaan</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:zoogdieren.html>zoogdieren</a>)</span>, <i>(taxonomisch)</i> <a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Papio" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Papio"><span style="color:green;"><i>Papio</i></span></a> <img alt="op Wikispecies" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/14px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png" decoding="async" width="14" height="18" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/21px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/28px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 2x" data-file-width="125" data-file-height="160" />, <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aap.html>aap</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:korte.html>korte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:staart.html>staart</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> vooruitstekende <a href = vnd.unilang:snuit.html>snuit</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i>In <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dierentuin.html>dierentuin</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waren.html>waren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verschillende.html>verschillende</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:soorten.html>soorten</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bavianen.html>bavianen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bezichtigen.html>bezichtigen</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***bazar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bazar.html>bazar</a> (95492)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bazaar</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">bazaar</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:bazar.html>bazar</a></i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:bazar.html>bazar</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ottoman_Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ottoman Turkish language">Ottoman Turkish</a></span> <i class="ota-Arab mention" lang="ota">بازار</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ota-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bâzâr</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">بازار</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bâzâr</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="id">pasar</i>.

***bazuin.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bazuin.html>bazuin</a> (35334)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Early Modern Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">basuyne</i> (1599), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">basune</i> (1399), <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">busine</i> (1240), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">buisine</i> (± 1080)<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">būcina</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bazuin.html>bazuin</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bazuinen.html>bazuinen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bazuin.html>bazuintje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>buisine, mediaeval trumpet</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> only used to denote the historical instrument that consisted of a simple straight metal tube, on which only natural harmonics could be produced.</li></ul>

***beaker.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beaker.html>beaker</a> (119578)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">bekyr</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">biker</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">bikarr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cup</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">bikeri</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cup</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">bīcārium</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wine <a href = vnd.unilang:vat.html>vat</a>, jug</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, of disputed origin. Possibly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">βῖκος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bîkos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">earthenware jug, wine jar</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">bacarium</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wine <a href = vnd.unilang:vat.html>vat</a>, vase</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian language">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq">Bieker</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mug, cup, <a href = vnd.unilang:beaker.html>beaker</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beker.html>beker</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:beaker.html>beaker</a>, cup</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Becher</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:beaker.html>beaker</a>, cup, <a href = vnd.unilang:goblet.html>goblet</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">bæger</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:beaker.html>beaker</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">bicchiere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cup, glass (for <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a>)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">pitcher</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:beaker.html>beaker</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">beakers</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A flat-bottomed vessel, with a lip, used as a laboratory container.</li>
<li>A drinking vessel without a handle, sometimes for the use of children.</li>
<li>A mug.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Antarctica" class="extiw" title="w:Antarctica">Antarctica</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A scientist.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2008</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:kim.html>Kim</a> Stanley Robinson,  <cite>Antarctica</cite>, page 52:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> at every meal break he shambled into the galley black-fingered and smelling of engine-grease and concrete floors, to contemplate <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> his meal the <b>beakers</b> at their round tables chatting away, completely oblivious <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***beamen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beamen.html>beamen</a> (23579)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">beamenen</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:amen.html>amen</a></i>, with the final <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-enen</i> simplified to just <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beamen.html>beamen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to say, reply '<a href = vnd.unilang:amen.html>amen</a>' after an uttering, notably in prayer or liturgy (especially in a responsory)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to assent to a statement</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">beamenen</span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beamer.html>beamer</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">beaming</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">beam</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beamen.html>beamen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to (transport by) beam; mainly used in science fiction context
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Scotty <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meester.html>meester</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:beamen.html>beamen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Enterprise.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Scotty <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a master at <b>beaming</b> to and from the Enterprise.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***beanie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beanie.html>beanie</a> (45856)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bean</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">the head</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:-ie.html>-ie</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:beanie.html>beanie</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">beanies</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A cap that fits the head closely, usually knitted from wool.
<dl><dd><i>Enrique Iglesias <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> often seen wearing a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:beanie.html>beanie</a></b>.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>A head-hugging brimless cap, with or without a visor, made from triangular sections of cloth, leather, or silk joined by a button at the crown and seamed together around the sides.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Beanie_Baby" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Beanie Baby"><a href = vnd.unilang:beanie.html>Beanie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:baby.html>Baby</a></a>, a small soft toy filled with <a href = vnd.unilang:beans.html>beans</a> or similar stuffing.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">cap</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">knit cap</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">knit hat</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">skull cap</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">skullie</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">skully</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">snow cap</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">snow hat</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">ski cap</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">sock cap</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">stocking cap</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Canada</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">watch cap</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">woolly hat</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">UK</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">wooly hat</span></li></ul>
</body>

***beck.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beck.html>beck</a> (8012)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:bek.html>bek</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">bekk</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">becc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">bekkr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a stream or brook</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bakiz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stream</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:bek.html>bek</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:beck.html>beck</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Bach</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beek.html>beek</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">bæc</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:bec.html>bec</a></i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">bæċe</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">beċe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:beck.html>beck</a>, brook</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">batch</i>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">beach</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:beck.html>beck</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:becks.html>becks</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norfolk" class="extiw" title="w:Norfolk">Norfolk</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> Northern English dialect</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A stream or small river.
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by Drayton and provide title, author's full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd>The brooks, the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:becks.html>becks</a></b>, the rills.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1976</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Archie_Fisher" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Archie Fisher"><a href = vnd.unilang:archie.html>Archie</a> Fisher</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:lyrics.html>lyrics</a> and music),  “The Witch Of The West-Mer-Lands”, in  <cite>The <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>Man</a> With A Rhyme</cite>, Sharon, CT |  Folk Legacy Records:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:beck.html>Beck</a></b> water cold and clear, will never clean your wound</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">brook</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">burn</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">creek</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">stream</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:bekken.html>bekken</a></i>, a shortened form of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">bekenen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">bēcnan</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">bēacnian</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to signify; beckon</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*baukną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">beacon</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">beacon</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:beck.html>beck</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:becks.html>becks</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A significant nod, or motion of the head or hand, especially as a call or command.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1671</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Milton" class="extiw" title="w:John Milton">John Milton</a>,  “Book the Second”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paradise_Regained" class="extiw" title="w:Paradise Regained">Paradise Regain’d. M[acock] for John Starkey<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="at the Mitre in Fleetstreet, near Temple-Bar">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/228732398">228732398</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://archive.org/stream/paradiseregaindp00milt_0page/n9/mode/1up">page 40</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Then forthwith to him <a href = vnd.unilang:takes.html>takes</a> a choſen <a href = vnd.unilang:band.html>band</a> / Of <a href = vnd.unilang:spirits.html>Spirits</a> likeſt to himſelf in <a href = vnd.unilang:guile.html>guile</a> / To be at hand, and at his <b><a href = vnd.unilang:beck.html>beck</a></b> appear,</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To nod or motion with the head.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:becket.html>becket</a> (47805)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bek.html>bek</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">beak</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> beak, and English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">beak</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:becket.html>becket</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">beckets</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A short piece of rope spliced to form a circle</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:loop.html>loop</a> of rope with a knot at one end to catch in an eye at the other end<sup id="cite_ref-FM5501_1-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-FM5501-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>. Used to secure oars etc. at their place.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sewing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:loop.html>loop</a> of thread, typically braided, attached at each end to a jacket. Used to pass through the brooch <a href = vnd.unilang:bar.html>bar</a> of medals to affix them to the jacket without damaging it.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The clevis of a pulley block.</li>
<li>An eye in the end of a rope.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A pocket in clothing.
<ul><li><b>1855</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:augustus.html>Augustus</a> Wise, <i>Tales for the Marines</i> (page 121)
<dl><dd>At the same time, mind, I must have a bit of a frolic occasionally, for that's all the pleasure I <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a>, when I <a href = vnd.unilang:gets.html>gets</a> a little <a href = vnd.unilang:chink.html>chink</a> in my <b><a href = vnd.unilang:becket.html>becket</a></b>; and ye know, too, that I don <a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> care much for that stuff, for a <a href = vnd.unilang:dollar.html>dollar</a> goes with <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> as fur as a gold ounce does with you, when ye put on your grand <a href = vnd.unilang:airs.html>airs</a>, and shower it about like a nabob.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A method of joining fabric, for example the <a href = vnd.unilang:doors.html>doors</a> of a <a href = vnd.unilang:tent.html>tent</a>, by interlacing <a href = vnd.unilang:loops.html>loops</a> of cord (<i>beckets</i>) through eyelet <a href = vnd.unilang:holes.html>holes</a> and adjacent <a href = vnd.unilang:loops.html>loops</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialect</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A spade for digging turf.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Wright to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bedekken.html>bedekken</a> (8864)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bedecken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">bithekken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*biþakjaną</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dekken.html>dekken</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bethatch</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">bedecken</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">betäcka</i>.

***bedel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bedel.html>bedel</a> (39815)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedelen.html>bedelen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedel.html>bedel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedel.html>bedels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedel.html>bedeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A charm <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">small trinket or pendant on a bracelet</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li>The practice of begging, mendicancy.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>In the sense “charm” most commonly used in the diminutive form <i><a href = vnd.unilang:bedel.html>bedeltje</a></i>. When used as the first component in a compound noun, however, as in <i>bedelarmband</i> = <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedel.html>bedel</a></strong></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:armband.html>armband</a></i>, the main form <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">begging</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gebedel.html>gebedel</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">begging</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedelen.html>bedelen</a></span></li></ul>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Pedell</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">bidellus</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">bedellus</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pedellus</i>.

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A beadle, academic usher.</li></ol>

***bedelaar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bedelaar.html>bedelaar</a> (12713)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bēdelāre</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedelen.html>bedelen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to beg</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-aar</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedelaar.html>bedelaar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedelaars.html>bedelaars</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedelaartje.html>bedelaartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">bedelares</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A beggar, a mendicant, who requests alms or handouts.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schooier.html>schooier</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:pauper.html>pauper</a>, one who can'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> properly provide in his/her own/family's needs.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:armoedzaaier.html>armoedzaaier</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pauper.html>pauper</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schooier.html>schooier</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bedelen.html>bedelen</a> (11518)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bēdelen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bedalon</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bidden.html>bidden</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-elen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:delen.html>delen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to divide, to share</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedelen.html>bedelen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to assign, to attribute, to impart, to endow [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a></i> <span>(object)</span></span> = with]
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>Zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:genen.html>genen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bedeelden.html>bedeelden</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:scherp.html>scherp</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verstand.html>verstand</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:afstamming.html>afstamming</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bedeelde.html>bedeelde</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niettemin.html>niettemin</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:slavernij.html>slavernij</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">His genes <b>endowed</b> him with a sharp <a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a>, his descent nevertheless <b>stuck</b> him with slavery.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to divide, portion</li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b>bedélen</b>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedelstaf.html>bedelstaf</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedelstaf.html>bedelstaven</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A beggar's cane.
<ul><li><b>1940</b>, Leonhard Huizinga, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:olivier.html>Olivier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> Adriaan</i>, 1971 ed., page 58.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:volgde.html>volgde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voorbeeld.html>voorbeeld</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zwijgend.html>zwijgend</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wandelden.html>wandelden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wij.html>wij</a> geruime <a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voort.html>voort</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zwaar.html>zwaar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:steunend.html>steunend</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onze.html>onze</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bedelstaf.html>bedelstaven</a></b>.</span><dl><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this quote)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> destitution, deep poverty.</li></ol>

***bedenken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bedenken.html>bedenken</a> (1732)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedenken.html>bedenken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bithenkan</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bithenkon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*biþankijaną</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:denken.html>denken</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedenken.html>bedenken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bethink</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to think of, to make up</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to reconsider, to change one's mind</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The reflexive form <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a different meaning, but <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> sometimes used with the same meaning as the non-reflexive form. This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> marked.
</p>

***bediende.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bediende.html>bediende</a> (4386)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inflected form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bediend.html>bediend</a></i>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Bedienter</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bediende.html>bediende</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedienden.html>bedienden</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bediendes.html>bediendes</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bediende.html>bediendetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>servant, low-ranking employee <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">any gender</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> employee
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:werknemer.html>werknemer</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>The plural <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bediendes.html>bediendes</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> only used to indicate multiple female servants. Use the word <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedienden.html>bedienden</a></i> for a group of male servants or for a group of mixed gender.
</p>

***bedienen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bedienen.html>bedienen</a> (6072)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedienen.html>bedienen</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dienen.html>dienen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedienen.html>bedienen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be of assistance to, to serve</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bediening.html>bediening</a> (11822)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedienen.html>bedienen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">serve, operate, handle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ing, -ance, -tion</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bediening.html>bediening</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedieningen.html>bedieningen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bediening.html>bedieninkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>attendance, service</li>
<li>maintenance, service</li>
